The code derived from the given problem is formed by interleaving the split digits of each paper. 

**Step-by-step Explanation:**

1. **Identify Split Digits:**
   - **Paper1:** Left-ripped after the first digit splits into [5, 2].
   - **Paper2:** Right-ripped before the last digit splits into [1, 4].

2. **Interleave the Split Digits:**
   - Alternate digits from Paper1 and Paper2 starting with Paper1's split.
   - Sequence becomes 5 (from Paper1), 1 (from Paper2), 2 (from Paper1), 4 (from Paper2).

3. **Form the Code:**
   - Combine the interleaved digits to get 5124.
